-- 导出  表 basketball_ticket_system.admin 结构
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `admin` (
  `admin_id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '管理员ID',
  `username` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '管理员账号',
  `password` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '密码',
  `real_name` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '真实姓名',
  `role` enum('SUPER_ADMIN','TICKET_ADMIN','USER_ADMIN') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'TICKET_ADMIN' COMMENT '管理员角色',
  `phone` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '手机号',
  `email` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '邮箱',
  `status` enum('ACTIVE','INACTIVE') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'ACTIVE' COMMENT '状态',
  `last_login_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '最后登录时间',
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`admin_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `username` (`username`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=17 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='管理员表';

-- 导出  表 basketball_ticket_system.admin_log 结构
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `admin_log` (
  `log_id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '日志ID',
  `admin_id` bigint NOT NULL COMMENT '管理员ID',
  `admin_name` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '管理员姓名',
  `action` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '操作动作',
  `module` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '操作模块',
  `target_id` bigint DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '操作目标ID',
  `details` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT '操作详情',
  `ip_address` varchar(45) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '操作IP',
  `user_agent` varchar(500) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '用户代理',
  `operation_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '操作时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`log_id`),
  KEY `idx_admin_id` (`admin_id`),
  KEY `idx_module` (`module`),
  KEY `idx_operation_time` (`operation_time`),
  CONSTRAINT `admin_log_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`admin_id`) REFERENCES `admin` (`admin_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=21 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='管理员日志表';

-- 导出  表 basketball_ticket_system.matchrecord 结构
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `matchrecord` (
  `match_id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '赛事ID',
  `match_name` varchar(200) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '赛事名称',
  `home_team` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '主队',
  `away_team` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '客队',
  `venue` varchar(200) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '比赛场馆',
  `match_time` datetime NOT NULL COMMENT '比赛时间',
  `description` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT '赛事描述',
  `total_seats` int NOT NULL COMMENT '总座位数',
  `available_seats` int NOT NULL COMMENT '可用座位数',
  `base_price` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL COMMENT '基础票价',
  `status` enum('UPCOMING','ONGOING','FINISHED','CANCELLED') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'UPCOMING' COMMENT '赛事状态',
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`match_id`),
  KEY `idx_match_time` (`match_time`),
  KEY `idx_status` (`status`),
  KEY `idx_teams` (`home_team`,`away_team`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=9 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='赛事表';

-- 导出  表 basketball_ticket_system.orders 结构
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `orders` (
  `order_id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '订单ID',
  `order_number` varchar(64) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '订单编号',
  `user_id` bigint NOT NULL COMMENT '用户ID',
  `match_id` bigint NOT NULL COMMENT '赛事ID',
  `total_amount` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL COMMENT '订单总金额',
  `actual_amount` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL COMMENT '实际支付金额',
  `seat_count` int NOT NULL COMMENT '座位数量',
  `order_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '下单时间',
  `pay_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '支付时间',
  `expire_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '订单过期时间',
  `status` enum('PENDING','PAID','CANCELLED','REFUNDED','EXPIRED') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'PENDING' COMMENT '订单状态',
  `pay_method` enum('WECHAT','ALIPAY','BANK_CARD') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '支付方式',
  `transaction_id` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '支付交易号',
  `refund_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '退款时间',
  `refund_amount` decimal(10,2) DEFAULT '0.00' COMMENT '退款金额',
  `refund_reason` varchar(500) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '退款原因',
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`order_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `order_number` (`order_number`),
  KEY `idx_user_id` (`user_id`),
  KEY `idx_match_id` (`match_id`),
  KEY `idx_order_time` (`order_time`),
  KEY `idx_status` (`status`),
  KEY `idx_order_number` (`order_number`),
  CONSTRAINT `orders_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`user_id`) REFERENCES `user` (`user_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `orders_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`match_id`) REFERENCES `matchrecord` (`match_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=37 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='订单表';

-- 导出  表 basketball_ticket_system.order_seat 结构
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `order_seat` (
  `id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '关联ID',
  `order_id` bigint NOT NULL COMMENT '订单ID',
  `seat_id` bigint NOT NULL COMMENT '座位ID',
  `price` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL COMMENT '购买时的价格',
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uk_order_seat` (`order_id`,`seat_id`),
  KEY `idx_order_id` (`order_id`),
  KEY `idx_seat_id` (`seat_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `order_seat_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`order_id`) REFERENCES `orders` (`order_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE,
  CONSTRAINT `order_seat_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`seat_id`) REFERENCES `seat` (`seat_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=107 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='订单座位关联表';

-- 导出  表 basketball_ticket_system.seat 结构
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `seat` (
  `seat_id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '座位ID',
  `match_id` bigint NOT NULL COMMENT '赛事ID',
  `seat_number` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '座位号（如：A区1排10座）',
  `seat_zone` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '区域（如：A区）',
  `seat_row` int NOT NULL COMMENT '排号',
  `seat_col` int NOT NULL COMMENT '列号',
  `seat_type` enum('STANDARD','VIP','PREMIUM') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'STANDARD' COMMENT '座位类型',
  `price` decimal(10,2) NOT NULL COMMENT '实际价格',
  `is_booked` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '0' COMMENT '是否已预订',
  `is_available` tinyint(1) DEFAULT '1' COMMENT '是否可用',
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  `order_id` bigint DEFAULT NULL,
  PRIMARY KEY (`seat_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `uk_match_seat` (`match_id`,`seat_number`),
  KEY `idx_match_id` (`match_id`),
  KEY `idx_seat_status` (`is_booked`,`is_available`),
  CONSTRAINT `seat_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`match_id`) REFERENCES `matchrecord` (`match_id`) ON DELETE CASCADE
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=2401 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='座位表';

-- 导出  表 basketball_ticket_system.system_config 结构
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `system_config` (
  `config_id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '配置ID',
  `config_key` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '配置键',
  `config_value` text COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '配置值',
  `config_desc` varchar(200) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '配置描述',
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`config_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `config_key` (`config_key`),
  KEY `idx_config_key` (`config_key`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=5 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='系统配置表';

-- 导出  表 basketball_ticket_system.tickets 结构
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `tickets` (
  `ticket_id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '电子票ID',
  `ticket_number` varchar(64) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '票号',
  `order_id` bigint NOT NULL COMMENT '订单ID',
  `seat_id` bigint NOT NULL COMMENT '座位ID',
  `qr_code` varchar(500) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '二维码数据',
  `check_status` enum('UNCHECKED','CHECKED') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'UNCHECKED' COMMENT '检票状态',
  `check_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '检票时间',
  `check_operator` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '检票操作员',
  `issue_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '出票时间',
  `status` enum('VALID','USED','REFUNDED','EXPIRED') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'VALID' COMMENT '票状态',
  `create_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '创建时间',
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`ticket_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `ticket_number` (`ticket_number`),
  KEY `idx_order_id` (`order_id`),
  KEY `idx_ticket_number` (`ticket_number`),
  KEY `idx_check_status` (`check_status`),
  KEY `seat_id` (`seat_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `tickets_ibfk_1` FOREIGN KEY (`order_id`) REFERENCES `orders` (`order_id`),
  CONSTRAINT `tickets_ibfk_2` FOREIGN KEY (`seat_id`) REFERENCES `seat` (`seat_id`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=26 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='电子票表';

-- 导出  表 basketball_ticket_system.user 结构
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS `user` (
  `user_id` bigint NOT NULL AUTO_INCREMENT COMMENT '用户ID',
  `username` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '用户名',
  `password` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci NOT NULL COMMENT '密码（加密存储）',
  `email` varchar(100) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '邮箱',
  `phone` varchar(20) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '手机号',
  `real_name` varchar(50) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '真实姓名',
  `id_card` varchar(18) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '身份证号',
  `role` enum('USER','ADMIN') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'USER' COMMENT '用户角色',
  `status` enum('ACTIVE','BANNED') COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT 'ACTIVE' COMMENT '账号状态',
  `avatar_url` varchar(255) COLLATE utf8mb4_unicode_ci DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '头像URL',
  `register_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '注册时间',
  `last_login_time` datetime DEFAULT NULL COMMENT '最后登录时间',
  `update_time` datetime DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP ON UPDATE CURRENT_TIMESTAMP COMMENT '更新时间',
  PRIMARY KEY (`user_id`),
  UNIQUE KEY `username` (`username`),
  UNIQUE KEY `email` (`email`),
  KEY `idx_username` (`username`),
  KEY `idx_phone` (`phone`),
  KEY `idx_email` (`email`)
) ENGINE=InnoDB AUTO_INCREMENT=24 DEFAULT CHARSET=utf8mb4 COLLATE=utf8mb4_unicode_ci COMMENT='用户表';
